  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6faaffe7-25cf-4b29-b66f-5e8e199a821f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/363696-1-">من أسوء ما قرأت للآسباب الاتية 
1- حستنى أنها حلقة من حلقات محمد حسان 
2- مفروض أن هذه الرواية تهدف إلى دعوة غير المسلمين للإسلام فبتقولهم الكاتبة أن غير المسلم سيدخل النار يسلم على أسلب الدعوة الرائع 
3- ان الرواية لم تطرح أى قضايا جدلية مهمة عن الإسلام تثير الرغبة عند المسلم وغير المسلم للبحث والنقاش ?</a>
</div>

<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/12179179-esraa"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1345819712i/12179179._UX100_CR0,16,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/12179179-esraa">Esraa</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">أولا الروايه دى زودت حبى أنا نفسى فى دينى ما بالك بغيرالمسلمين ، كمان قدمتالإسلام بصورة بسيطة عجبتنى جداً و ناقشت قضايا مهمة زى قضية الحجاب وفرضه بطري<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">أولا الروايه دى زودت حبى أنا نفسى فى دينى ما بالك بغيرالمسلمين ، كمان قدمتالإسلام بصورة بسيطة عجبتنى جداً و ناقشت قضايا مهمة زى قضية الحجاب وفرضه بطريقة عجبتنى جداً وعملت مقارنة بين الأديان التلاتة فى النقطة دى بشكل حلو بردوا .<br />ثانيا: مين قال أن الرواية هدفها دعوت غير المسلمين للإسلام ؟؟ الكاتبة نفسها مقلتش كدة .. كل ما فى الأمر أنها سمعت قصة أثرت فيها فقررت تعرضها لكن فى محتوى درامى حفاظاً على صاحبة القصة الحقيقية ... وبس :)<br /> <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

However, I was amazed by the sequence of events and the easiness of style that I enjoyed it more because it revolves around religion and politics, and not just romance.   <span id="freeText6072197948115435586" style="display:none">I was very reluctant to start such novel simply because I don't want to read about religion nor politics. However, I was amazed by the sequence of events and the easiness of style that I enjoyed it more because it revolves around religion and politics, and not just romance. It portrayed the similarities between Islam, Christianity and Judaism. With an emphasis on the fact that people should judge the religion and its principles rather than its practitioners who may be flawed by false prejudices and intolerant views. I was entertained by the converting process of the characters. It was not done in vein, but supported by strong arguments and evidences. Moreover, the romantic part of the novel was thrilling, simple, and captivating.<br />In simple words, I loved it and I wish I would've read it sooner.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3322233220" />
    <a title="Farah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69538834-farah"><img alt="Farah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601159556p2/69538834.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69538834-farah?shelf=my-recommendations">my-recommendations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69538834-farah?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69538834-farah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69538834-farah?shelf=arabic-books">arabic-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69538834-farah?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3322233220" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5913268461935116628">This is my second time reading this book, I am lucky enough that the first time I read it was 3-4 years ago, so I could feel ALMOST everything once again.<br/>This review contains spoilers. <br/>I want to mention my favorite character or shall I say person as it was mentioned that this was based on a true story.<br/>Reema.<br/>She was so angelic, how she would sacrifice everything she has, her shelter, Jacob's hugs and compassion when she knew she would lose it all for the sake of what she believed in.<br/>It is not her</span>
  <span id="freeText5913268461935116628" style="display:none">This is my second time reading this book, I am lucky enough that the first time I read it was 3-4 years ago, so I could feel ALMOST everything once again.<br />This review contains spoilers. <br />I want to mention my favorite character or shall I say person as it was mentioned that this was based on a true story.<br />Reema.<br />She was so angelic, how she would sacrifice everything she has, her shelter, Jacob's hugs and compassion when she knew she would lose it all for the sake of what she believed in.<br />It is not her only death that made me wipe my waterfall of tears, it was also her journey, Rachel's husband and his verbal and literal abuse, her favorite person who she is basically thought of him as her father, Sonia and her bullying, poor Reema she didn't even tell anyone what she had to go through, she never complained.<br />She did things that normally us muslims are free to do, no risks, yet we don't.<br />I wish that killing her was part of the drama that the author had to add, and that she is still somewhere inspiring people just like she inspired me. Despite how young she was, she knew what the most important things were. And if sadly this was true, that she died, I hope that her soul rest in peace.<br />I loved Nada and Ahmed's love story, it wasn't just a normal one. It was based on wanting their significant other to be better. I kinda wished their was a deeper reason for why he lost his memories, but wow Hassan, you made me hate you so well.<br />To be honest, it was a little unrealistic for me that almost all jew mentioned converted to islam, tho it did indeed warm my heart. <br />Reema was the sun in this novel, she radiated her beliefs, purity and innocence, and eventually it reached everyone. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5913268461935116628" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1286138495" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1286138495" />
    <a title="Mariam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2410659-mariam"><img alt="Mariam" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1286138495?book_show_action=true">May 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mariam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mariam" href="/user/show/2410659-mariam">Mariam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1286138495" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17836704718131458541">I am not sure exactly how to rate this book overall but I will state what I liked and disliked about the book:<br/><br/>Liked:<br/>1) The idea itself is very nice and touches on the Arabic society of mixed religions in a very nice and realistic way. The interactions of the communities together and the nature of each community are brought to life...<br/>2) The historical atmosphere of the Lebanon war and the reactions of the characters to these events are also real and quite deep.<br/>3) Each character had a distinct per</span>
  <span id="freeText17836704718131458541" style="display:none">I am not sure exactly how to rate this book overall but I will state what I liked and disliked about the book:<br /><br />Liked:<br />1) The idea itself is very nice and touches on the Arabic society of mixed religions in a very nice and realistic way. The interactions of the communities together and the nature of each community are brought to life...<br />2) The historical atmosphere of the Lebanon war and the reactions of the characters to these events are also real and quite deep.<br />3) Each character had a distinct personality. You almost feel like you know these people in real life.<br />4) The book was very emotional and moving.<br />5) It is nice to see an "innocent" romance kind of book where the protagonists fall madly in love without actually touching each other even once during the whole book. That is a big plus compared to modern Arabic novels.<br /><br />Disliked:<br />1) The plot was taken from the aconventional zone to a very standard worn-out plot. It is a typical Arabic movie plot only with a touch of a message or an idea that the author wanted to convey. I would have liked it more had the plot ended in a more realistic way by actually Nada moving on with her life.. After learning what she learned from Ahmed, he could have simply remained a symbol rather than returning like what happens in so many Arabic movies and I could name many of them!<br /><br />2) HONEST POINT: Anyone who is not a Muslim and reads this book will see that the author is obviously biased. <br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17836704718131458541" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I am sick and tired of a portraying Muslim women as some obedient, oppressed-looking creatures with their head fully covered and looking down. The face of the Muslim-looking woman on the cover is the source of light in the cover and her dreaming eyes are looking way up (most probably) to the sky, which is a novelty.</span>

<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9753375"><img alt="أرض زيكولا" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1441287700l/9753375._SX98_.jpg" />

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eun3OHJjVvK9L51UIthz0uYXllF0drL7o39aWdxR4B+pW4qNh1eecJjbv/QGwULPduIoE2V8BXtkT7EKJ+cJxQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9PPJDkMtyRDup1v+ceweuPfFIh9Jwm1kLIXs7hYdzvYnQbS7thkBkstTeV5V9S+lZzCcXVjI2uTrtQe97asnLA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
